<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/pɛn/</span>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/pin%E2%80%93pen_merger" class="extiw" title="w:pin–pen merger"><i>pin</i>–<i>pen</i> merger</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/pɪn/</span></li></ul></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/pen#Middle_English" title="pen">pen</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/penne#Middle_English" title="penne">penne</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enclosure for animals</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/penn#Old_English" title="penn">penn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enclosure, fold, pen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (in compounds), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/penn%C5%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/pennō (page does not exist)">*pennō</a></i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/pannij%C5%8D&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Germanic/pannijō (page does not exist)">*pannijō</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pin, bolt, nail, tack</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/bend-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/bend- (page does not exist)">*bend-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pointed peg, nail, edge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/w/index.php?title=pennian&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="pennian (page does not exist)">pennian</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to close, lock, bolt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (in compounds <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/w/index.php?title=onpennian&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="onpennian (page does not exist)">onpennian</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to open</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href="/wiki/pennen#Low_German" title="pennen">pennen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to secure a door with a bolt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/pinn#Old_English" title="pinn">pinn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peg, bolt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pin#English" title="pin">pin</a></i>.
</p><p>Sense “prison” originally figurative extension to “enclosure for persons” (1845), later influenced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/penitentiary#English" title="penitentiary">penitentiary</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">prison</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, being analyzed as an abbreviation (1884).<sup id="cite_ref-oetyld_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-oetyld-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pen</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pens#English" title="pens">pens</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An <a href="/wiki/enclosure" title="enclosure">enclosure</a> (<a href="/wiki/enclose" title="enclose">enclosed</a> area) used to contain <a href="/wiki/domesticated" title="domesticated">domesticated</a> animals, especially <a href="/wiki/sheep" title="sheep">sheep</a> or <a href="/wiki/cattle" title="cattle">cattle</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">There are two steers in the third <b>pen</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/prison" title="prison">prison</a> <a href="/wiki/cell" title="cell">cell</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">They caught him with a stolen horse, and he wound up in the <b>pen</b> again.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/baseball" title="baseball">baseball</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href="/wiki/bullpen" title="bullpen">bullpen</a>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Two righties are up in the <b>pen</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pen</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pens#English" title="pens">pens</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/penning#English" title="penning">penning</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/penned#English" title="penned">penned</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pent#English" title="pent">pent</a></b>)

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Etymology 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ballpoint-pen-parts.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Ballpoint-pen-parts.jpg/220px-Ballpoint-pen-parts.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="125" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Ballpoint-pen-parts.jpg/330px-Ballpoint-pen-parts.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fd/Ballpoint-pen-parts.jpg/440px-Ballpoint-pen-parts.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="568"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ballpoint-pen-parts.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>A <a href="/wiki/ballpoint_pen" title="ballpoint pen">ballpoint pen</a>, showing assembly.</div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/penne#Middle_English" title="penne">penne</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/penne#Old_French" title="penne">penne</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href="/wiki/penne#Old_French" title="penne">penne</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href="/wiki/penna#Latin" title="penna">penna</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">feather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/p%C3%A9th%E2%82%82r%CC%A5" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/péth₂r̥">*péth₂r̥ ~ pth₂én-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">feather, wing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/peth%E2%82%82-" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/peth₂-">*peth₂-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rush, fly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from which <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/petition#English" title="petition">petition</a></i>). Proto-Indo-European base also root of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/petra-&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Indo-European/petra- (page does not exist)">*petra-</a></i>, from which <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%CF%80%CF%84%CE%B5%CF%81%CF%8C%CE%BD#Ancient_Greek" title="πτερόν">πτερόν</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pterón</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (whence <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pterodactyl#English" title="pterodactyl">pterodactyl</a></i>), Sanskrit <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa"><a href="/w/index.php?title=patram&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="patram (page does not exist)">पत्रम्</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">patram</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wing, feather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href="/wiki/%D0%BF%D0%B5%D1%80%D0%BE#Old_Church_Slavonic" title="перо">перо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pero</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pen</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href="/wiki/fj%C7%AB%C3%B0r#Old_Norse" title="fjǫðr">fjǫðr</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/w/index.php?title=fe%C3%B0er&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="feðer (page does not exist)">feðer</a></i> (Modern English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/feather#English" title="feather">feather</a></i>);<sup id="cite_ref-oetyld_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-oetyld-1">[1]</a></sup> note the /p/ → /f/ Germanic sound change.
</p><p>See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/feather#English" title="feather">feather</a></i> and <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc"><a href="/wiki/%CF%80%CE%AD%CF%84%CE%BF%CE%BC%CE%B1%CE%B9#Ancient_Greek" title="πέτομαι">πέτομαι</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pétomai</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for more.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pen</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pens#English" title="pens">pens</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A tool, originally made from a <a href="/wiki/feather" title="feather">feather</a> but now usually a small tubular instrument, containing ink used to <a href="/wiki/write" title="write">write</a> or make marks.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He took notes with a <b>pen</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figuratively</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A writer, or his style.
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He has a sharp <b>pen</b>.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(Can we <a href="/wiki/Category:Requests_for_date" title="Category:Requests for date">date</a> this quote?)</span>,  Fuller, <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(Please provide the book title or journal name)</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">those learned <b>pens</b></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#colloquial" title="Appendix:Glossary">colloquial</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Marks of ink left by a pen.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He's unhappy because he got <b>pen</b> on his new shirt.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/light_pen" title="light pen">light pen</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/zoology" title="zoology">zoology</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The internal <a href="/wiki/cartilage" title="cartilage">cartilage</a> skeleton of a <a href="/wiki/squid" title="squid">squid</a>, shaped like a pen.
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b>,  Danna Staaf,  <cite>Squid Empire</cite>, ForeEdge, <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9781611689235" title="Special:BookSources/9781611689235">→ISBN</a></small>, page 117:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">A <b>pen</b> is nothing more complex than a decalcified shell, so one mutation of the genes that controlled calcification could be all it took.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now rare<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/poetic" title="poetic">poetic</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#dialectal" title="Appendix:Glossary">dialectal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/feather" title="feather">feather</a>, especially one of the flight feathers of a bird, angel etc.
<span class="HQToggle"><a>quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1590</b>,  Edmund Spenser,  <cite>The Faerie Queene</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And eke the <b>pennes</b>, that did his pineons bynd, / Were like mayne-yards, with flying canuas lynd, / With which whenas him list the ayre to beat <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/poetic" title="poetic">poetic</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/wing" title="wing">wing</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: #777777;">(Can we <a href="/wiki/Category:Requests_for_quotation/Milton" title="Category:Requests for quotation/Milton">find and add</a> a quotation of Milton to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pen</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pens#English" title="pens">pens</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/penning#English" title="penning">penning</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/penned#English" title="penned">penned</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/write" title="write">write</a> (an article, a book, etc.).</li></ol>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">pen</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/pens#English" title="pens">pens</a></b>)

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href="/wiki/penne#Middle_Dutch" title="penne">penne</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Etymology" title="Wiktionary:Etymology">etymology</a> is incomplete. <h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_4">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_9">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="id">pèn</strong> (<i>plural</i>, <i>first-person possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="id">pen<a href="/wiki/-ku#Indonesian" title="-ku">ku</a></b>, <i>second-person possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="id">pen<a href="/wiki/-mu#Indonesian" title="-mu">mu</a></b>, <i>third-person possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="id">pen<a href="/wiki/-nya#Indonesian" title="-nya">nya</a></b>)

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Romanization_2">Romanization</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Romanization">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Nonstandard spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="cmn"><a href="/wiki/p%C4%93n#Mandarin" title="pēn">pēn</a></i></span></span>.</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Nonstandard spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="cmn"><a href="/wiki/p%C3%A9n#Mandarin" title="pén">pén</a></i></span></span>.</li>

<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Nonstandard spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="cmn"><a href="/wiki/p%C3%A8n#Mandarin" title="pèn">pèn</a></i></span></span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>English <a href="/wiki/transcription" title="transcription">transcriptions</a> of Mandarin speech often fail to distinguish between the critical <a href="/wiki/tonal" title="tonal">tonal</a> differences employed in the Mandarin language, using words such as this one without the appropriate indication of tone.</li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Welsh">Welsh</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=91" title="Edit section: Welsh">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_11">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=pen&amp;action=edit&amp;section=92" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Welsh" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Welsh">Middle Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="wlm"><a href="/wiki/penn#Middle_Welsh" title="penn">penn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brittonic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Brittonic languages">Proto-Brythonic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-bry-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Brythonic/penn" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Brythonic/penn">*penn</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/k%CA%B7ennom" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Celtic/kʷennom">*kʷennom</a></i>.
